In [2]:
import functools                                                                                                                                            
print = functools.partial(print, flush=True)
import shlex, sys                                                                                                                                           
                                                                                                                                                          
def run(command: str):                                                                                                                                      
  parts = shlex.split(command)                          
  name = parts[0].replace("-", "_")
  module = __import__(f"neural_search.cli.{name}", fromlist=["main"])                                                                                     
  old_argv = sys.argv
  try:                                                                                                                                                    
      sys.argv = parts                                  
      module.main()                                                                                                                                       
  finally:
      sys.argv = old_argv

def compare(query):
    print("ns")
    run("search-neural '"+ query +"' --tokenizer data/tokenizer.json --chunks data/chunks.jsonl --checkpoint checkpoints/encoder.pt --device cuda")
    print("bm25")
    run("bm25-search '"+query+"' --chunks data/chunks.jsonl")

compare("attention mechanism in transformers")
compare("multi-head attention")
compare("hidden markov model")
compare("HMM")
compare("named entity recognition")
compare("beam search decoding")
compare("chomsky normal form")
compare("viterbi algorithm")
